These panes all have their\n39:  * own instance of the {@code Trigger}.\n40:  *\n41:  * <p>Triggers must not maintain state internally since they can be re-created or reused for\n42:  * different keys. `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/triggers/Trigger.java` — Studied abstract Trigger interface and TriggerContext methods\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/windows/TimeWindow.java` — Analyzed TimeWindow structure (start, end, maxTimestamp)\n\n## Dependency Chain\n\n1. **Define TradingSessionExtractor interface** — Functional interface, models SessionWindowTimeGapExtractor\n2. **Implement PricingSessionWindow assigner** — Extends MergingWindowAssigner<Object, TimeWindow>, calculates session boundaries based on trading hours\n3. **Implement PricingSessionTrigger** — Extends Trigger<Object, TimeWindow>, fires at market close\n4. **Integration** — Both components work together using EventTimeTrigger.create() pattern and TimeWindow.mergeWindows()\n\n## Architecture Notes\n\n### Window Assignment Strategy\n- **Input**: Market ID, timezone, open/close times (LocalTime)\n- **Processing**: For each element timestamp, determine which trading session it belongs to\n- **Output**: TimeWindow with session open/close timestamps\n- **Merging**: Delegates to TimeWindow.mergeWindows() for handling overlapping windows\n\n### Trigger Strategy\n- Fires when watermark passes window.maxTimestamp() (end of trading session)\n- Supports configurable early firing (circuit breaker events)\n- Implements canMerge() = true and onMerge() for session window compatibility\n- Clears event-time timers on window destruction\n\n## Implementation Strategy\n\n### PricingSessionExtractor (Functional Interface)\n```\nSignature: long extract(T element)\nPurpose: Extract market identifier from stream elements\nPackage: org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.assigners\nFollows: SessionWindowTimeGapExtractor pattern\n```\n\n### PricingSessionWindow (MergingWindowAssigner)\n```\nConstructor: PricingSessionWindow(String marketId, ZoneId timezone, LocalTime open, LocalTime close)\nKey Methods:\n- assignWindows(): Calculate TimeWindow for given element timestamp\n- getDefaultTrigger(): Return EventTimeTrigger.create()\n- mergeWindows(): Delegate to TimeWindow.mergeWindows()\n- getWindowSerializer(): Return new TimeWindow.Serializer()\n- isEventTime(): Return true\n\nHelper Method:\n- forMarket(String marketId, ZoneId timezone, LocalTime open, LocalTime close): Static factory\n\nLogic:\n1. Convert element timestamp to trading session date in market timezone\n2. Create window boundaries: [sessionStart, sessionEnd]\n3. Handle overnight sessions (e.g., futures markets)\n4. Return window as single-element collection\n```\n\n### PricingSessionTrigger (Trigger)\n```\nConstructor: Private, accessed via create() static method\nKey Methods:\n- onElement(): Register timer for window.maxTimestamp() if watermark not past\n- onEventTime(): Fire when time == window.maxTimestamp()\n- onProcessingTime(): Continue (event-time only)\n- clear(): Delete registered event-time timer\n- canMerge(): Return true\n- onMerge(): Re-register timer if watermark hasn't passed merged window end\n\nLogic:\n- Extends EventTimeTrigger pattern\n- Fires at session end when watermark arrives\n- Supports configurable early triggers via overridable onElement()\n```\n\n## Key Design Decisions\n\n1. **Using TimeWindow**: Maintains compatibility with existing Flink infrastructure, merging logic, serialization\n2. **Event-Time Based**: Financial trading operates on event time (market time), not processing time\n3. **Extending MergingWindowAssigner**: Allows overlapping session windows to be merged automatically\n4. **Delegating Merge to TimeWindow.mergeWindows()**: Reuses robust existing merge logic\n5. **EventTimeTrigger Pattern**: Simple, proven trigger strategy that fires at session boundaries\n6. **Factory Method**: Provides clean API (PricingSessionWindow.forMarket(...))\n\n## Testing Approach\n- Verify window assignment for various market timezones (NYSE, LSE, Asia-Pacific)\n- Test overnight session handling (futures markets)\n- Verify window merging behavior with overlapping sessions\n- Test trigger firing at session boundaries\n- Validate watermark handling and late-arriving elements\n\n## Files to Create\n\n1. `/workspace/flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/TradingSessionExtractor.java`\n2. timer\n- canMerge(): Return true\n- onMerge(): Re-register timer if watermark hasn't passed merged window end\n\nLogic:\n- Extends EventTimeTrigger pattern\n- Fires at session end when watermark arrives\n- Supports configurable early triggers via overridable onElement()\n```\n\n## Key Design Decisions\n\n1. **Using TimeWindow**: Maintains compatibility with existing Flink infrastructure, {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01Fg43Qo3nYTSK18UfPvGng8","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01RXzQBKYwqaWEw1EiVwhfbA","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/PricingSessionWindow.java","content":"/*\n * Licensed to the Apache Software Foundation (ASF) under one\n * or more contributor license agreements.  See the NOTICE file\n * distributed with this work for additional information\n * regarding copyright ownership.  The ASF licenses this file\n * to you under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the\n * \"License\"); you may not use this file except in compliance\n * with the License.  You may obtain a copy of the License at\n *\n *     http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0\n *\n * Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software\n * distributed under the License is distributed on an \"AS IS\" BASIS,\n * WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.\n * See the License for the specific language governing permissions and\n * limitations under the License.\n */\n\npackage org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.assigners;\n\nimport org.apache.flink.annotation.PublicEvolving;\nimport org.apache.flink.api.common.ExecutionConfig;\nimport org.apache.flink.api.common.typeutils.TypeSerializer;\nimport org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.triggers.EventTimeTrigger;\nimport org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.triggers.Trigger;\nimport org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.windows.TimeWindow;\n\nimport java.time.LocalTime;\nimport java.time.ZoneId;\nimport java.time.ZonedDateTime;\nimport java.util.Collection;\nimport java.util.Collections;\n\n/**\n * A {@link WindowAssigner} that windows trading events into sessions based on market trading\n * hours. Windows are defined by market open and close times, allowing for session-based\n * aggregations in financial streaming applications.\n *\n * <p>For example, to create a session window for NYSE (09:30-16:00 ET):\n *\n * <pre>{@code\n * DataStream<PriceEvent> prices = ...;\n * KeyedStream<PriceEvent, String> keyed = prices.keyBy(e -> e.symbol);\n * WindowedStream<PriceEvent, String, TimeWindow> windowed =\n *   keyed.window(PricingSessionWindow.forMarket(\n *       \"NYSE\",\n *       ZoneId.of(\"America/New_York\"),\n *       LocalTime.of(9, 30),\n *       LocalTime.of(16, 0)\n *   ));\n * }</pre>\n */\n@PublicEvolving\npublic class PricingSessionWindow extends MergingWindowAssigner<Object, TimeWindow> {\n    private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;\n\n    private final String marketId;\n    private final ZoneId timezone;\n    private final LocalTime sessionOpen;\n    private final LocalTime sessionClose;\n\n    protected PricingSessionWindow(\n            String marketId, ZoneId timezone, LocalTime sessionOpen, LocalTime sessionClose) {\n        if (marketId == null || marketId.isEmpty()) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Market ID cannot be null or empty\");\n        }\n        if (timezone == null) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Timezone cannot be null\");\n        }\n        if (sessionOpen == null || sessionClose == null) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Session open and close times cannot be null\");\n        }\n\n        this.marketId = marketId;\n        this.timezone = timezone;\n        this.sessionOpen = sessionOpen;\n        this.sessionClose = sessionClose;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Collection<TimeWindow> assignWindows(\n            Object element, long timestamp, WindowAssignerContext context) {\n        // Convert timestamp to market timezone\n        ZonedDateTime eventDateTime = ZonedDateTime.ofInstant(\n                java.time.Instant.ofEpochMilli(timestamp), timezone);\n\n        // Calculate session start and end timestamps\n        ZonedDateTime sessionStartZdt =\n                eventDateTime.toLocalDate().atTime(sessionOpen).atZone(timezone);\n        ZonedDateTime sessionEndZdt =\n                eventDateTime.toLocalDate().atTime(sessionClose).atZone(timezone);\n\n        long sessionStartMs = sessionStartZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n        long sessionEndMs = sessionEndZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n\n        // If event is before session open, assign to previous session\n        if (timestamp < sessionStartMs) {\n            sessionStartZdt = sessionStartZdt.minusDays(1);\n            sessionEndZdt = sessionEndZdt.minusDays(1);\n            sessionStartMs = sessionStartZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n            sessionEndMs = sessionEndZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n        }\n        // If event is after session close, assign to next session\n        else if (timestamp >= sessionEndMs) {\n            sessionStartZdt = sessionStartZdt.plusDays(1);\n            sessionEndZdt = sessionEndZdt.plusDays(1);\n            sessionStartMs = sessionStartZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n            sessionEndMs = sessionEndZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n        }\n\n        return Collections.singletonList(new TimeWindow(sessionStartMs, sessionEndMs));\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Trigger<Object, TimeWindow> getDefaultTrigger() {\n        return EventTimeTrigger.create();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        return String.format(\n                \"PricingSessionWindow(%s, %s, %s-%s)\",\n                marketId, timezone, sessionOpen, sessionClose);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a new {@code PricingSessionWindow} that assigns elements to sessions based on a\n     * fixed market's trading hours.\n     *\n     * @param marketId The market identifier (e.g., \"NYSE\", \"LSE\")\n     * @param timezone The timezone in which the market operates\n     * @param open The market opening time\n     * @param close The market closing time\n     * @return The window assigner\n     */\n    public static PricingSessionWindow forMarket(\n            String marketId, ZoneId timezone, LocalTime open, LocalTime close) {\n        return new PricingSessionWindow(marketId, timezone, open, close);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public TypeSerializer<TimeWindow> getWindowSerializer(ExecutionConfig executionConfig) {\n        return new TimeWindow.Serializer();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean isEventTime() {\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    /** Merge overlapping {@link TimeWindow}s. */\n    @Override\n    public void mergeWindows(\n            Collection<TimeWindow> windows, MergingWindowAssigner.MergeCallback<TimeWindow> c) {\n        TimeWindow.mergeWindows(windows, c);\n Windows are defined by market open and close times, allowing for session-based\n * aggregations in financial streaming applications.\n *\n * <p>For example, to create a session window for NYSE (09:30-16:00 ET):\n *\n * <pre>{@code\n * DataStream<PriceEvent> prices = ...;\n * KeyedStream<PriceEvent, String> keyed = prices.keyBy(e -> e.symbol);\n * WindowedStream<PriceEvent, String, TimeWindow> windowed =\n *   keyed.window(PricingSessionWindow.forMarket(\n *       \"NYSE\",\n *       ZoneId.of(\"America/New_York\"),\n *       LocalTime.of(9, 30),\n *       LocalTime.of(16, 0)\n *   ));\n * }</pre>\n */\n@PublicEvolving\npublic class PricingSessionWindow extends MergingWindowAssigner<Object, TimeWindow> {\n    private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;\n\n    private final String marketId;\n    private final ZoneId timezone;\n    private final LocalTime sessionOpen;\n    private final LocalTime sessionClose;\n\n    protected PricingSessionWindow(\n            String marketId, ZoneId timezone, LocalTime sessionOpen, LocalTime sessionClose) {\n        if (marketId == null || marketId.isEmpty()) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Market ID cannot be null or empty\");\n        }\n        if (timezone == null) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Timezone cannot be null\");\n        }\n        if (sessionOpen == null || sessionClose == null) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Session open and close times cannot be null\");\n        }\n\n        this.marketId = marketId;\n        this.timezone = timezone;\n        this.sessionOpen = sessionOpen;\n        this.sessionClose = sessionClose;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Collection<TimeWindow> assignWindows(\n            Object element, long timestamp, WindowAssignerContext context) {\n        // Convert timestamp to market timezone\n        ZonedDateTime eventDateTime = ZonedDateTime.ofInstant(\n                java.time.Instant.ofEpochMilli(timestamp), timezone);\n\n        // Calculate session start and end timestamps\n        ZonedDateTime sessionStartZdt =\n                eventDateTime.toLocalDate().atTime(sessionOpen).atZone(timezone);\n        ZonedDateTime sessionEndZdt =\n                eventDateTime.toLocalDate().atTime(sessionClose).atZone(timezone);\n\n        long sessionStartMs = sessionStartZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n        long sessionEndMs = sessionEndZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n\n        // If event is before session open, assign to previous session\n        if (timestamp < sessionStartMs) {\n            sessionStartZdt = sessionStartZdt.minusDays(1);\n            sessionEndZdt = sessionEndZdt.minusDays(1);\n            sessionStartMs = sessionStartZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n            sessionEndMs = sessionEndZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n        }\n        // If event is after session close, assign to next session\n        else if (timestamp >= sessionEndMs) {\n            sessionStartZdt = sessionStartZdt.plusDays(1);\n            sessionEndZdt = sessionEndZdt.plusDays(1);\n            sessionStartMs = sessionStartZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n            sessionEndMs = sessionEndZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n        }\n\n        return Collections.singletonList(new TimeWindow(sessionStartMs, sessionEndMs));\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Trigger<Object, TimeWindow> getDefaultTrigger() {\n        return EventTimeTrigger.create();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        return String.format(\n                \"PricingSessionWindow(%s, %s, %s-%s)\",\n                marketId, timezone, sessionOpen, sessionClose);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a new {@code PricingSessionWindow} that assigns elements to sessions based on a\n     * fixed market's trading hours.\n     *\n     * @param marketId The market identifier (e.g., \"NYSE\", \"LSE\")\n     * @param timezone The timezone in which the market operates\n     * @param open The market opening time\n     * @param close The market closing time\n     * @return The window assigner\n     */\n    public static PricingSessionWindow forMarket(\n            String marketId, ZoneId timezone, LocalTime open, LocalTime close) {\n        return new PricingSessionWindow(marketId, timezone, open, close);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public TypeSerializer<TimeWindow> getWindowSerializer(ExecutionConfig executionConfig) {\n        return new TimeWindow.Serializer();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean isEventTime() {\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    /** Merge overlapping {@link TimeWindow}s. */\n    @Override\n    public void mergeWindows(\n            Collection<TimeWindow> windows, MergingWindowAssigner.MergeCallback<TimeWindow> c) {\n        TimeWindow.mergeWindows(windows, c);\n    }\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

Windows are defined by market open and close times, allowing for session-based\n    37→ * aggregations in financial streaming applications.\n    38→ *\n    39→ * <p>For example, to create a session window for NYSE (09:30-16:00 ET):\n    40→ *\n    41→ * <pre>{@code\n    42→ * DataStream<PriceEvent> prices = ...;\n    43→ * KeyedStream<PriceEvent, String> keyed = prices.keyBy(e -> e.symbol);\n    44→ * WindowedStream<PriceEvent, String, TimeWindow> windowed =\n    45→ *   keyed.window(PricingSessionWindow.forMarket(\n    46→ *       \"NYSE\",\n    47→ *       ZoneId.of(\"America/New_York\"),\n    48→ *       LocalTime.of(9, 30),\n    49→ *       LocalTime.of(16, 0)\n    50→ *   ));\n    51→ * }</pre>\n    52→ */\n    53→@PublicEvolving\n    54→public class PricingSessionWindow extends MergingWindowAssigner<Object, TimeWindow> {\n    55→    private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;\n    56→\n    57→    private final String marketId;\n    58→    private final ZoneId timezone;\n    59→    private final LocalTime sessionOpen;\n    60→    private final LocalTime sessionClose;\n    61→\n    62→    protected PricingSessionWindow(\n    63→            String marketId, ZoneId timezone, LocalTime sessionOpen, LocalTime sessionClose) {\n    64→        if (marketId == null || marketId.isEmpty()) {\n    65→            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Market ID cannot be null or empty\");\n    66→        }\n    67→        if (timezone == null) {\n    68→            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Timezone cannot be null\");\n    69→        }\n    70→        if (sessionOpen == null || sessionClose == null) {\n    71→            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Session open and close times cannot be null\");\n    72→        }\n    73→\n    74→        this.marketId = marketId;\n    75→        this.timezone = timezone;\n    76→        this.sessionOpen = sessionOpen;\n    77→        this.sessionClose = sessionClose;\n    78→    }\n    79→\n    80→    @Override\n    81→    public Collection<TimeWindow> assignWindows(\n    82→            Object element, long timestamp, WindowAssignerContext context) {\n    83→        // Convert timestamp to market timezone\n    84→        ZonedDateTime eventDateTime = ZonedDateTime.ofInstant(\n    85→                java.time.Instant.ofEpochMilli(timestamp), timezone);\n    86→\n    87→        // Calculate session start and end timestamps\n    88→        ZonedDateTime sessionStartZdt =\n    89→                eventDateTime.toLocalDate().atTime(sessionOpen).atZone(timezone);\n    90→        ZonedDateTime sessionEndZdt =\n    91→                eventDateTime.toLocalDate().atTime(sessionClose).atZone(timezone);\n    92→\n    93→        long sessionStartMs = sessionStartZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n    94→        long sessionEndMs = sessionEndZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n    95→\n    96→        // If event is before session open, assign to previous session\n    97→        if (timestamp < sessionStartMs) {\n    98→            sessionStartZdt = sessionStartZdt.minusDays(1);\n    99→            sessionEndZdt = sessionEndZdt.minusDays(1);\n   100→            sessionStartMs = sessionStartZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n   101→            sessionEndMs = sessionEndZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n   102→        }\n   103→        // If event is after session close, assign to next session\n   104→        else if (timestamp >= sessionEndMs) {\n   105→            sessionStartZdt = sessionStartZdt.plusDays(1);\n   106→            sessionEndZdt = sessionEndZdt.plusDays(1);\n   107→            sessionStartMs = sessionStartZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n   108→            sessionEndMs = sessionEndZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n   109→        }\n   110→\n   111→        return Collections.singletonList(new TimeWindow(sessionStartMs, sessionEndMs));\n   112→    }\n   113→\n   114→    @Override\n   115→    public Trigger<Object, TimeWindow> getDefaultTrigger() {\n   116→        return EventTimeTrigger.create();\n   117→    }\n   118→\n   119→    @Override\n   120→    public String toString() {\n   121→        return String.format(\n   122→                \"PricingSessionWindow(%s, %s, %s-%s)\",\n   123→                marketId, timezone, sessionOpen, sessionClose);\n   124→    }\n   125→\n   126→    /**\n   127→     * Creates a new {@code PricingSessionWindow} that assigns elements to sessions based on a\n   128→     * fixed market's trading hours.\n   129→     *\n   130→     * @param marketId The market identifier (e.g., \"NYSE\", \"LSE\")\n   131→     * @param timezone The timezone in which the market operates\n   132→     * @param open The market opening time\n   133→     * @param close The market closing time\n   134→     * @return The window assigner\n   135→     */\n   136→    public static PricingSessionWindow forMarket(\n   137→            String marketId, ZoneId timezone, LocalTime open, LocalTime close) {\n   138→        return new PricingSessionWindow(marketId, timezone, open, close);\n   139→    }\n   140→\n   141→    @Override\n   142→    public TypeSerializer<TimeWindow> getWindowSerializer(ExecutionConfig executionConfig) {\n   143→        return new TimeWindow.Serializer();\n   144→    }\n   145→\n   146→    @Override\n   147→    public boolean isEventTime() {\n   148→        return true;\n   149→    }\n   150→\n   151→    /** Merge overlapping {@link TimeWindow}s. */\n   152→    @Override\n   153→    public void mergeWindows(\n   154→            Collection<TimeWindow> windows, MergingWindowAssigner.MergeCallback<TimeWindow> c) {\n   155→        TimeWindow.mergeWindows(windows, c);\n   156→    }\n   157→}\n   158→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should Windows are defined by market open and close times, allowing for session-based\n * aggregations in financial streaming applications.\n *\n * <p>For example, to create a session window for NYSE (09:30-16:00 ET):\n *\n * <pre>{@code\n * DataStream<PriceEvent> prices = ...;\n * KeyedStream<PriceEvent, String> keyed = prices.keyBy(e -> e.symbol);\n * WindowedStream<PriceEvent, String, TimeWindow> windowed =\n *   keyed.window(PricingSessionWindow.forMarket(\n *       \"NYSE\",\n *       ZoneId.of(\"America/New_York\"),\n *       LocalTime.of(9, 30),\n *       LocalTime.of(16, 0)\n *   ));\n * }</pre>\n */\n@PublicEvolving\npublic class PricingSessionWindow extends MergingWindowAssigner<Object, TimeWindow> {\n    private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;\n\n    private final String marketId;\n    private final ZoneId timezone;\n    private final LocalTime sessionOpen;\n    private final LocalTime sessionClose;\n\n    protected PricingSessionWindow(\n            String marketId, ZoneId timezone, LocalTime sessionOpen, LocalTime sessionClose) {\n        if (marketId == null || marketId.isEmpty()) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Market ID cannot be null or empty\");\n        }\n        if (timezone == null) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Timezone cannot be null\");\n        }\n        if (sessionOpen == null || sessionClose == null) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Session open and close times cannot be null\");\n        }\n\n        this.marketId = marketId;\n        this.timezone = timezone;\n        this.sessionOpen = sessionOpen;\n        this.sessionClose = sessionClose;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Collection<TimeWindow> assignWindows(\n            Object element, long timestamp, WindowAssignerContext context) {\n        // Convert timestamp to market timezone\n        ZonedDateTime eventDateTime = ZonedDateTime.ofInstant(\n                java.time.Instant.ofEpochMilli(timestamp), timezone);\n\n        // Calculate session start and end timestamps\n        ZonedDateTime sessionStartZdt =\n                eventDateTime.toLocalDate().atTime(sessionOpen).atZone(timezone);\n        ZonedDateTime sessionEndZdt =\n                eventDateTime.toLocalDate().atTime(sessionClose).atZone(timezone);\n\n        long sessionStartMs = sessionStartZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n        long sessionEndMs = sessionEndZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n\n        // If event is before session open, assign to previous session\n        if (timestamp < sessionStartMs) {\n            sessionStartZdt = sessionStartZdt.minusDays(1);\n            sessionEndZdt = sessionEndZdt.minusDays(1);\n            sessionStartMs = sessionStartZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n            sessionEndMs = sessionEndZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n        }\n        // If event is after session close, assign to next session\n        else if (timestamp >= sessionEndMs) {\n            sessionStartZdt = sessionStartZdt.plusDays(1);\n            sessionEndZdt = sessionEndZdt.plusDays(1);\n            sessionStartMs = sessionStartZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n            sessionEndMs = sessionEndZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n        }\n\n        return Collections.singletonList(new TimeWindow(sessionStartMs, sessionEndMs));\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Trigger<Object, TimeWindow> getDefaultTrigger() {\n        return EventTimeTrigger.create();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        return String.format(\n                \"PricingSessionWindow(%s, %s, %s-%s)\",\n                marketId, timezone, sessionOpen, sessionClose);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a new {@code PricingSessionWindow} that assigns elements to sessions based on a\n     * fixed market's trading hours.\n     *\n     * @param marketId The market identifier (e.g., \"NYSE\", \"LSE\")\n     * @param timezone The timezone in which the market operates\n     * @param open The market opening time\n     * @param close The market closing time\n     * @return The window assigner\n     */\n    public static PricingSessionWindow forMarket(\n            String marketId, ZoneId timezone, LocalTime open, LocalTime close) {\n        return new PricingSessionWindow(marketId, timezone, open, close);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public TypeSerializer<TimeWindow> getWindowSerializer(ExecutionConfig executionConfig) {\n        return new TimeWindow.Serializer();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean isEventTime() {\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    /** Merge overlapping {@link TimeWindow}s. */\n    @Override\n    public void mergeWindows(\n            Collection<TimeWindow> windows, MergingWindowAssigner.MergeCallback<TimeWindow> c) {\n        TimeWindow.mergeWindows(windows, c);\n    }\n}\n","numLines":158,"startLine":1,"totalLines":158}}}

See the NOTICE file\n * distributed with this work for additional information\n * regarding copyright ownership.  The ASF licenses this file\n * to you under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the\n * \"License\"); you may not use this file except in compliance\n * with the License.  You may obtain a copy of the License at\n *\n *     http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0\n *\n * Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software\n * distributed under the License is distributed on an \"AS IS\" BASIS,\n * WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.\n * See the License for the specific language governing permissions and\n * limitations under the License.\n */\n\npackage org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.assigners;\n\nimport org.apache.flink.annotation.PublicEvolving;\nimport org.apache.flink.api.common.ExecutionConfig;\nimport org.apache.flink.api.common.typeutils.TypeSerializer;\nimport org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.triggers.EventTimeTrigger;\nimport org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.triggers.Trigger;\nimport org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.windows.TimeWindow;\n\nimport java.time.LocalTime;\nimport java.time.ZoneId;\nimport java.time.ZonedDateTime;\nimport java.util.Collection;\nimport java.util.Collections;\n\n/**\n * A {@link WindowAssigner} that windows trading events into sessions based on market trading\n * hours. Windows are defined by market open and close times, allowing for session-based\n * aggregations in financial streaming applications.\n */\n@PublicEvolving\npublic class PricingSessionWindow extends MergingWindowAssigner<Object, TimeWindow> {\n    private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;\n\n    private final String marketId;\n    private final ZoneId timezone;\n    private final LocalTime sessionOpen;\n    private final LocalTime sessionClose;\n\n    protected PricingSessionWindow(\n            String marketId, ZoneId timezone, LocalTime sessionOpen, LocalTime sessionClose) {\n        if (marketId == null || marketId.isEmpty()) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Market ID cannot be null or empty\");\n        }\n        if (timezone == null) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Timezone cannot be null\");\n        }\n        if (sessionOpen == null || sessionClose == null) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Session open and close times cannot be null\");\n        }\n\n        this.marketId = marketId;\n        this.timezone = timezone;\n        this.sessionOpen = sessionOpen;\n        this.sessionClose = sessionClose;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Collection<TimeWindow> assignWindows(\n            Object element, long timestamp, WindowAssignerContext context) {\n        // Convert timestamp to market timezone\n        ZonedDateTime eventDateTime = ZonedDateTime.ofInstant(\n                java.time.Instant.ofEpochMilli(timestamp), timezone);\n\n        // Calculate session start and end timestamps\n        ZonedDateTime sessionStartZdt =\n                eventDateTime.toLocalDate().atTime(sessionOpen).atZone(timezone);\n        ZonedDateTime sessionEndZdt =\n                eventDateTime.toLocalDate().atTime(sessionClose).atZone(timezone);\n\n        long sessionStartMs = sessionStartZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n        long sessionEndMs = sessionEndZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n\n        // If event is before session open, assign to previous session\n        if (timestamp < sessionStartMs) {\n            sessionStartZdt = sessionStartZdt.minusDays(1);\n            sessionEndZdt = sessionEndZdt.minusDays(1);\n            sessionStartMs = sessionStartZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n            sessionEndMs = sessionEndZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n        }\n        // If event is after session close, assign to next session\n        else if (timestamp >= sessionEndMs) {\n            sessionStartZdt = sessionStartZdt.plusDays(1);\n            sessionEndZdt = sessionEndZdt.plusDays(1);\n            sessionStartMs = sessionStartZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n            sessionEndMs = sessionEndZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n        }\n\n        return Collections.singletonList(new TimeWindow(sessionStartMs, sessionEndMs));\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Trigger<Object, TimeWindow> getDefaultTrigger() {\n        return EventTimeTrigger.create();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        return String.format(\n                \"PricingSessionWindow(%s, %s, %s-%s)\",\n                marketId, timezone, sessionOpen, sessionClose);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a new {@code PricingSessionWindow} that assigns elements to sessions based on a\n     * fixed market's trading hours.\n     *\n     * @param marketId The market identifier (e.g., \"NYSE\", \"LSE\")\n     * @param timezone The timezone in which the market operates\n     * @param open The market opening time\n     * @param close The market closing time\n     * @return The window assigner\n     */\n    public static PricingSessionWindow forMarket(\n            String marketId, ZoneId timezone, LocalTime open, LocalTime close) {\n        return new PricingSessionWindow(marketId, timezone, open, close);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public TypeSerializer<TimeWindow> getWindowSerializer(ExecutionConfig executionConfig) {\n        return new TimeWindow.Serializer();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean isEventTime() {\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    /** Merge overlapping {@link TimeWindow}s. */\n    @Override\n    public void mergeWindows(\n            Collection<TimeWindow> windows, MergingWindowAssigner.MergeCallback<TimeWindow> c) {\n        TimeWindow.mergeWindows(windows, c);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/triggers/PricingSessionTrigger.java\n```java\n/*\n * Licensed to the Apache Software Foundation (ASF) under one\n * or more contributor license agreements.  See the NOTICE file\n * distributed with this work for additional information\n * regarding copyright ownership.  The ASF licenses this file\n * to you under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the\n * \"License\"); you may not use this file except in compliance\n * with the License.  You may obtain a copy of the License at\n *\n *     http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0\n *\n * Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software\n * distributed under the License is distributed on an \"AS IS\" BASIS,\n * WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.\n * See the License for the specific language governing permissions and\n * limitations under the License.\n */\n\npackage org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.triggers;\n\nimport org.apache.flink.annotation.PublicEvolving;\nimport org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.windows.TimeWindow;\n\n/**\n * A {@link Trigger} that fires when the market close time is reached (watermark passes the end of\n * the trading session window). This trigger is designed for use with {@link\n * org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.assigners.PricingSessionWindow} to fire trading\n * session aggregations at market close.\n */\n@PublicEvolving\npublic class PricingSessionTrigger extends Trigger<Object, TimeWindow> {\n    private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;\n\n    private PricingSessionTrigger() {}\n\n    @Override\n    public TriggerResult onElement(\n            Object element, long timestamp, TimeWindow window, TriggerContext ctx)\n            throws Exception {\n        if (window.maxTimestamp() <= ctx.getCurrentWatermark()) {\n            return TriggerResult.FIRE;\n        } else {\n            ctx.registerEventTimeTimer(window.maxTimestamp());\n            return TriggerResult.CONTINUE;\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public TriggerResult onEventTime(long time, TimeWindow window, TriggerContext ctx) {\n        return time == window.maxTimestamp() ? TriggerResult.FIRE : TriggerResult.CONTINUE;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public TriggerResult onProcessingTime(long time, TimeWindow window, TriggerContext ctx)\n            throws Exception {\n        return TriggerResult.CONTINUE;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void clear(TimeWindow window, TriggerContext ctx) throws Exception {\n        ctx.deleteEventTimeTimer(window.maxTimestamp());\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean canMerge() {\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void onMerge(TimeWindow window, OnMergeContext ctx) {\n        long windowMaxTimestamp = window.maxTimestamp();\n        if (windowMaxTimestamp > ctx.getCurrentWatermark()) {\n            ctx.registerEventTimeTimer(windowMaxTimestamp);\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        return \"PricingSessionTrigger()\";\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a pricing session trigger that fires when the watermark passes the end of the\n     * trading session window.\n     *\n     * @return A new PricingSessionTrigger instance\n     */\n    public static PricingSessionTrigger create() {\n        return new PricingSessionTrigger();\n    }\n}\n```\n\n## This requires implementing three components:\n\n1. **TradingSessionExtractor** - Functional interface for extracting market ID\n2. **PricingSessionWindow** - Custom window assigner\n3. **PricingSessionTrigger** - Custom trigger for market sessions\n\n## Files Examined\n\n### Existing Window Implementations\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/windows/TimeWindow.java` — Analyzed TimeWindow structure (start, end, maxTimestamp)\n\n## Dependency Chain\n\n1. **Define TradingSessionExtractor interface** — Functional interface, models SessionWindowTimeGapExtractor\n2. **Implement PricingSessionWindow assigner** — Extends MergingWindowAssigner<Object, TimeWindow>, calculates session boundaries based on trading hours\n3. **Implement PricingSessionTrigger** — Extends Trigger<Object, TimeWindow>, fires at market close\n4. **Integration** — Both components work together using EventTimeTrigger.create() pattern and TimeWindow.mergeWindows()\n\n## Architecture Notes\n\n### Window Assignment Strategy\n- **Input**: Market ID, timezone, open/close times (LocalTime)\n- **Processing**: For each element timestamp, determine which trading session it belongs to\n- **Output**: TimeWindow with session open/close timestamps\n- **Merging**: Delegates to TimeWindow.mergeWindows() for handling overlapping windows\n\n### Trigger Strategy\n- Fires when watermark passes window.maxTimestamp() (end of trading session)\n- Supports configurable early firing (circuit breaker events)\n- Implements canMerge() = true and onMerge() for session window compatibility\n- Clears event-time timers on window destruction\n\n## Implementation Strategy\n\n### PricingSessionExtractor (Functional Interface)\n```\nSignature: long extract(T element)\nPurpose: Extract market identifier from stream elements\nPackage: org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.assigners\nFollows: SessionWindowTimeGapExtractor pattern\n```\n\n### PricingSessionWindow (MergingWindowAssigner)\n```\nConstructor: PricingSessionWindow(String marketId, ZoneId timezone, LocalTime open, LocalTime close)\nKey Methods:\n- assignWindows(): Calculate TimeWindow for given element timestamp\n- getDefaultTrigger(): Return EventTimeTrigger.create()\n- mergeWindows(): Delegate to TimeWindow.mergeWindows()\n- getWindowSerializer(): Return new TimeWindow.Serializer()\n- isEventTime(): Return true\n\nHelper Method:\n- forMarket(String marketId, ZoneId timezone, LocalTime open, LocalTime close): Static factory\n\nLogic:\n1. Convert element timestamp to trading session date in market timezone\n2. Create window boundaries: [sessionStart, sessionEnd]\n3. Handle overnight sessions (e.g., futures markets)\n4. Return window as single-element collection\n```\n\n### PricingSessionTrigger (Trigger)\n```\nConstructor: Private, accessed via create() static method\nKey Methods:\n- onElement(): Register timer for window.maxTimestamp() if watermark not past\n- onEventTime(): Fire when time == window.maxTimestamp()\n- onProcessingTime(): Continue (event-time only)\n- clear(): Delete registered event-time timer\n- canMerge(): Return true\n- onMerge(): Re-register timer if watermark hasn't passed merged window end\n\nLogic:\n- Extends EventTimeTrigger pattern\n- Fires at session end when watermark arrives\n- Supports configurable early triggers via overridable onElement()\n```\n\n## Key Design Decisions\n\n1. **Using TimeWindow**: Maintains compatibility with existing Flink infrastructure, merging logic, serialization\n2. **Event-Time Based**: Financial trading operates on event time (market time), not processing time\n3. **Extending MergingWindowAssigner**: Allows overlapping session windows to be merged automatically\n4. **Delegating Merge to TimeWindow.mergeWindows()**: Reuses robust existing merge logic\n5. **EventTimeTrigger Pattern**: Simple, proven trigger strategy that fires at session boundaries\n6. **Factory Method**: Provides clean API (PricingSessionWindow.forMarket(...))\n\n## Testing Approach\n- Verify window assignment for various market timezones (NYSE, LSE, Asia-Pacific)\n- Test overnight session handling (futures markets)\n- Verify window merging behavior with overlapping sessions\n- Test trigger firing at session boundaries\n- Validate watermark handling and late-arriving elements\n\n## Files to Create\n\n1. `/workspace/flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/TradingSessionExtractor.java`\n2. Windows are defined by market open and close times, allowing for session-based","+ * aggregations in financial streaming applications.","+ */","+@PublicEvolving","+public class PricingSessionWindow extends MergingWindowAssigner<Object, TimeWindow> {","+    private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;","+","+    private final String marketId;","+    private final ZoneId timezone;","+    private final LocalTime sessionOpen;","+    private final LocalTime sessionClose;","+","+    protected PricingSessionWindow(","+            String marketId, ZoneId timezone, LocalTime sessionOpen, LocalTime sessionClose) {","+        if (marketId == null || marketId.isEmpty()) {","+            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Market ID cannot be null or empty\");","+        }","+        if (timezone == null) {","+            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Timezone cannot be null\");","+        }","+        if (sessionOpen == null || sessionClose == null) {","+            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Session open and close times cannot be null\");","+        }","+","+        this.marketId = marketId;","+        this.timezone = timezone;","+        this.sessionOpen = sessionOpen;","+        this.sessionClose = sessionClose;","+    }","+","+    @Override","+    public Collection<TimeWindow> assignWindows(","+            Object element, long timestamp, WindowAssignerContext context) {","+        // Convert timestamp to market timezone","+        ZonedDateTime eventDateTime = ZonedDateTime.ofInstant(","+                java.time.Instant.ofEpochMilli(timestamp), timezone);","+","+        // Calculate session start and end timestamps","+        ZonedDateTime sessionStartZdt =","+                eventDateTime.toLocalDate().atTime(sessionOpen).atZone(timezone);","+        ZonedDateTime sessionEndZdt =","+                eventDateTime.toLocalDate().atTime(sessionClose).atZone(timezone);","+","+        long sessionStartMs = sessionStartZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();","+        long sessionEndMs = sessionEndZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();","+","+        // If event is before session open, assign to previous session","+        if (timestamp < sessionStartMs) {","+            sessionStartZdt = sessionStartZdt.minusDays(1);","+            sessionEndZdt = sessionEndZdt.minusDays(1);","+            sessionStartMs = sessionStartZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();","+            sessionEndMs = sessionEndZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();","+        }","+        // If event is after session close, assign to next session","+        else if (timestamp >= sessionEndMs) {","+            sessionStartZdt = sessionStartZdt.plusDays(1);","+            sessionEndZdt = sessionEndZdt.plusDays(1);","+            sessionStartMs = sessionStartZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();","+            sessionEndMs = sessionEndZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();","+        }","+","+        return Collections.singletonList(new TimeWindow(sessionStartMs, sessionEndMs));","+    }","+","+    @Override","+    public Trigger<Object, TimeWindow> getDefaultTrigger() {","+        return EventTimeTrigger.create();","+    }","+","+    @Override","+    public String toString() {","+        return String.format(","+                \"PricingSessionWindow(%s, %s, %s-%s)\",","+                marketId, timezone, sessionOpen, sessionClose);","+    }","+","+    /**","+     * Creates a new {@code PricingSessionWindow} that assigns elements to sessions based on a","+     * fixed market's trading hours.","+     *","+     * @param marketId The market identifier (e.g., \"NYSE\", \"LSE\")","+     * @param timezone The timezone in which the market operates","+     * @param open The market opening time","+     * @param close The market closing time","+     * @return The window assigner","+     */","+    public static PricingSessionWindow forMarket(","+            String marketId, ZoneId timezone, LocalTime open, LocalTime close) {","+        return new PricingSessionWindow(marketId, timezone, open, close);","+    }","+","+    @Override","+    public TypeSerializer<TimeWindow> getWindowSerializer(ExecutionConfig executionConfig) {","+        return new TimeWindow.Serializer();","+    }","+","+    @Override","+    public boolean isEventTime() {","+        return true;","+    }","+","+    /** Merge overlapping {@link TimeWindow}s. */","+    @Override","+    public void mergeWindows(","+            Collection<TimeWindow> windows, MergingWindowAssigner.MergeCallback<TimeWindow> c) {","+        TimeWindow.mergeWindows(windows, c);","+    }","+}","+```","+","+### flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/triggers/PricingSessionTrigger.java","+```java","+/*","+ * Licensed to the Apache Software Foundation (ASF) under one","+ * or more contributor license agreements.  See the NOTICE file","+ * distributed with this work for additional information","+ * regarding copyright ownership.  The ASF licenses this file","+ * to you under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the","+ * \"License\"); you may not use this file except in compliance","+ * with the License.  You may obtain a copy of the License at","+ *","+ *     http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0","+ *","+ * Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software","+ * distributed under the License is distributed on an \"AS IS\" BASIS,","+ * WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.","+ * See the License for the specific language governing permissions and","+ * limitations under the License.","+ */","+","+package org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.triggers;","+","+import org.apache.flink.annotation.PublicEvolving;","+import org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.windows.TimeWindow;","+","+/**","+ * A {@link Trigger} that fires when the market close time is reached (watermark passes the end of","+ * the trading session window). This trigger is designed for use with {@link","+ * org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.assigners.PricingSessionWindow} to fire trading","+ * session aggregations at market close.","+ */","+@PublicEvolving","+public class PricingSessionTrigger extends Trigger<Object, TimeWindow> {","+    private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;","+","+    private PricingSessionTrigger() {}","+","+    @Override","+    public TriggerResult onElement(","+            Object element, long timestamp, TimeWindow window, TriggerContext ctx)","+            throws Exception {","+        if (window.maxTimestamp() <= ctx.getCurrentWatermark()) {","+            return TriggerResult.FIRE;","+        } else {","+            ctx.registerEventTimeTimer(window.maxTimestamp());","+            return TriggerResult.CONTINUE;","+        }","+    }","+","+    @Override","+    public TriggerResult onEventTime(long time, TimeWindow window, TriggerContext ctx) {","+        return time == window.maxTimestamp() ? TriggerResult.FIRE : TriggerResult.CONTINUE;","+    }","+","+    @Override","+    public TriggerResult onProcessingTime(long time, TimeWindow window, TriggerContext ctx)","+            throws Exception {","+        return TriggerResult.CONTINUE;","+    }","+","+    @Override","+    public void clear(TimeWindow window, TriggerContext ctx) throws Exception {","+        ctx.deleteEventTimeTimer(window.maxTimestamp());","+    }","+","+    @Override","+    public boolean canMerge() {","+        return true;","+    }","+","+    @Override","+    public void onMerge(TimeWindow window, OnMergeContext ctx) {","+        long windowMaxTimestamp = window.maxTimestamp();","+        if (windowMaxTimestamp > ctx.getCurrentWatermark()) {","+            ctx.registerEventTimeTimer(windowMaxTimestamp);","+        }","+    }","+","+    @Override","+    public String toString() {","+        return \"PricingSessionTrigger()\";","+    }","+","+    /**","+     * Creates a pricing session trigger that fires when the watermark passes the end of the","+     * trading session window.","+     *","+     * @return A new PricingSessionTrigger instance","+     */","+    public static PricingSessionTrigger create() {","+        return new PricingSessionTrigger();","+    }","+}","+```","+","+## Files Created","+"," 1. `/workspace/flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/TradingSessionExtractor.java`"," 2. `/workspace/flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/PricingSessionWindow.java`"," 3. `/workspace/flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/triggers/PricingSessionTrigger.java`"]}],"userModified":false,"replaceAll":false}}

TradingSessionExtractor Interface\n- **Purpose**: Provides a functional interface for dynamic market identifier extraction\n- **Design**: Mirrors `SessionWindowTimeGapExtractor<T>` pattern for consistency\n- **Serializable**: Supports distributed processing by implementing Serializable\n- **Use Case**: Enables future dynamic session window variants that determine trading hours per element\n\n#### 2. PricingSessionWindow Assigner\n**Core Algorithm**:\n```\nFor each element with timestamp T:\n1. Convert T to market timezone ZonedDateTime\n2. Calculate session open/close times for T's date using LocalTime values\n3. Compare T against session boundaries:\n   - If T < sessionOpen: assign to previous day's session\n   - If sessionOpen <= T < sessionClose: assign to current session\n   - If T >= sessionClose: assign to next day's session\n4. Return TimeWindow(sessionStartMs, sessionEndMs)\n```\n\n**Key Implementation Details**:\n- Uses `java.time` API (Java 8+) for timezone-aware date/time handling\n- `ZonedDateTime.ofInstant()` converts millisecond timestamp to market timezone\n- Window boundaries calculated in market timezone, then converted back to UTC milliseconds\n- Sessions handle day boundaries correctly via `minusDays()` and `plusDays()`\n- Delegates merging to `TimeWindow.mergeWindows()` using MergingWindowAssigner callback\n\n**Type Safety**:\n- Generic type `<Object, TimeWindow>` matches EventTimeSessionWindows pattern\n- Maintains compatibility with existing window operators and serializers\n\n#### 3. PricingSessionTrigger\n**Firing Logic**:\n- Extends `Trigger<Object, TimeWindow>` for type consistency with window assigner\n- Fires ONLY when `watermark >= window.maxTimestamp()` (session end reached)\n- Returns FIRE when event-time timer matches window end exactly\n- Implements merging support (`canMerge() = true`) for overlapping session consolidation\n\n**Event-Time Focus**:\n- Registers `EventTimeTimer` for window.maxTimestamp() (session close)\n- Ignores processing time (returns CONTINUE in onProcessingTime)\n- Suitable for financial data where market time (event time) is authoritative\n\n**Watermark Optimization**:\n- Checks if watermark already past window end on element arrival (TriggerResult.FIRE)\n- Avoids registering timer if watermark has passed (prevents double-firing in onMerge)\n\n### Design Rationale\n\n1. **Timezone Awareness**: Financial markets operate on local time, requiring explicit timezone handling. Using `java.time` API ensures daylight saving time correctness.\n\n2. **Event-Time Only**: Stock exchanges operate on event time (market time), not processing time. The implementation correctly ignores processing time triggers.\n\n3. **Window Merging**: By extending `MergingWindowAssigner`, PricingSessionWindow supports merging of overlapping sessions (important for handling late-arriving data that bridges session boundaries).\n\n4. **Compatibility**: Uses existing `TimeWindow` and delegates to `TimeWindow.mergeWindows()` for consistency with Flink's window infrastructure.\n\n5. **Factory Methods**: `PricingSessionWindow.forMarket()` and `PricingSessionTrigger.create()` provide clean, builder-like APIs consistent with Flink conventions.\n\n### Integration with Flink Ecosystem\n\n**Windowing Pipeline**:\n```\nDataStream<PriceEvent>\n  .keyBy(symbol)\n  .window(PricingSessionWindow.forMarket(\"NYSE\", ZoneId.of(\"America/New_York\"), ...))\n  .trigger(PricingSessionTrigger.create())  // Optional, default is EventTimeTrigger\n  .aggregate(priceAggregator)\n```\n\n**Benefits**:\n- Automatic session detection based on market hours\n- Correct handling of overnight gaps (e.g., premarket at 7am ET)\n- Support for international markets with different timezones\n- Proper merging of windows when elements arrive out-of-order\n- Full compatibility with Flink's fault tolerance and state management\n\n### Testing Considerations\n\nKey test scenarios:\n1. **Session Boundary Crossing**: Events before open, during session, after close\n2. **Timezone Handling**: DST transitions, different market timezones\n3. **Overnight Sessions**: Futures markets with 23-hour sessions\n4. **Out-of-Order Arrival**: Window merging with late elements\n5. **Watermark Semantics**: Trigger firing at correct event-time boundaries\n\n### Potential Extensions\n\nThe implementation supports future enhancements:\n1. **Dynamic Sessions**: Create subclass using `TradingSessionExtractor` to vary hours per element\n2. **Holiday Handling**: Override `assignWindows()` to skip market holidays\n3. **Early Termination**: Override trigger's `onElement()` for circuit breaker halts\n4. **Multiple Sessions**: Support pre/post-market sessions in single Calculate session open/close times for T's date using LocalTime values\n3. Compare T against session boundaries:\n   - If T < sessionOpen: assign to previous day's session\n   - If sessionOpen <= T < sessionClose: assign to current session\n   - If T >= sessionClose: assign to next day's session\n4. Return TimeWindow(sessionStartMs, sessionEndMs)\n```\n\n**Key Implementation Details**:\n- Uses `java.time` API (Java 8+) for timezone-aware date/time handling\n- `ZonedDateTime.ofInstant()` converts millisecond timestamp to market timezone\n- Window boundaries calculated in market timezone, then converted back to UTC milliseconds\n- Sessions handle day boundaries correctly via `minusDays()` and `plusDays()`\n- Delegates merging to `TimeWindow.mergeWindows()` using MergingWindowAssigner callback\n\n**Type Safety**:\n- Generic type `<Object, TimeWindow>` matches EventTimeSessionWindows pattern\n- Maintains compatibility with existing window operators and serializers\n\n#### 3. PricingSessionTrigger\n**Firing Logic**:\n- Extends `Trigger<Object, TimeWindow>` for type consistency with window assigner\n- Fires ONLY when `watermark >= window.maxTimestamp()` (session end reached)\n- Returns FIRE when event-time timer matches window end exactly\n- Implements merging support (`canMerge() = true`) for overlapping session consolidation\n\n**Event-Time Focus**:\n- Registers `EventTimeTimer` for window.maxTimestamp() (session close)\n- Ignores processing time (returns CONTINUE in onProcessingTime)\n- Suitable for financial data where market time (event time) is authoritative\n\n**Watermark Optimization**:\n- Checks if watermark already past window end on element arrival (TriggerResult.FIRE)\n- Avoids registering timer if watermark has passed (prevents double-firing in onMerge)\n\n### Design Rationale\n\n1. **Timezone Awareness**: Financial markets operate on local time, requiring explicit timezone handling. Using `java.time` API ensures daylight saving time correctness.\n\n2. **Event-Time Only**: Stock exchanges operate on event time (market time), not processing time. The implementation correctly ignores processing time triggers.\n\n3. **Window Merging**: By extending `MergingWindowAssigner`, PricingSessionWindow supports merging of overlapping sessions (important for handling late-arriving data that bridges session boundaries).\n\n4. **Compatibility**: Uses existing `TimeWindow` and delegates to `TimeWindow.mergeWindows()` for consistency with Flink's window infrastructure.\n\n5. **Factory Methods**: `PricingSessionWindow.forMarket()` and `PricingSessionTrigger.create()` provide clean, builder-like APIs consistent with Flink conventions.\n\n### Integration with Flink Ecosystem\n\n**Windowing Pipeline**:\n```\nDataStream<PriceEvent>\n  .keyBy(symbol)\n  .window(PricingSessionWindow.forMarket(\"NYSE\", ZoneId.of(\"America/New_York\"), ...))\n  .trigger(PricingSessionTrigger.create())  // Optional, default is EventTimeTrigger\n  .aggregate(priceAggregator)\n```\n\n**Benefits**:\n- Automatic session detection based on market hours\n- Correct handling of overnight gaps (e.g., premarket at 7am ET)\n- Support for international markets with different timezones\n- Proper merging of windows when elements arrive out-of-order\n- Full compatibility with Flink's fault tolerance and state management\n\n### Testing Considerations\n\nKey test scenarios:\n1. **Session Boundary Crossing**: Events before open, during session, after close\n2. **Timezone Handling**: DST transitions, different market timezones\n3. **Overnight Sessions**: Futures markets with 23-hour sessions\n4. **Out-of-Order Arrival**: Window merging with late elements\n5. **Watermark Semantics**: Trigger firing at correct event-time boundaries\n\n### Potential Extensions\n\nThe implementation supports future enhancements:\n1. **Dynamic Sessions**: Create subclass using `TradingSessionExtractor` to vary hours per element\n2. **Holiday Handling**: Override `assignWindows()` to skip market holidays\n3. **Early Termination**: Override trigger's `onElement()` for circuit breaker halts\n4. **Multiple Sessions**: Support pre/post-market sessions in single market","originalFile":"# PricingSessionWindow Implementation Analysis\n\n## Task Overview\nImplement a custom `PricingSessionWindow` assigner for Apache Flink that groups trading events by market session boundaries rather than fixed time intervals. This requires implementing three components:\n\n1. **TradingSessionExtractor** - Functional interface for extracting market ID\n2. **PricingSessionWindow** - Custom window assigner\n3. **PricingSessionTrigger** - Custom trigger for market sessions\n\n## Files Examined\n\n### Existing Window Implementations\n- `flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/EventTimeSessionWindows.java` — Analyzed for basic session window pattern, extends MergingWindowAssigner<Object, TimeWindow>\n- `flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/DynamicEventTimeSessionWindows.java` — Examined for dynamic gap extraction pattern, supports element-based session computation\n- `flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/SessionWindowTimeGapExtractor.java` — Studied for functional interface pattern\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/WindowAssigner.java` — Understood base class interface requirements\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/MergingWindowAssigner.java` — Analyzed mergeWindows() callback pattern\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/triggers/EventTimeTrigger.java` — Examined trigger lifecycle: onElement(), onEventTime(), onMerge(), clear()\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/triggers/Trigger.java` — Studied abstract Trigger interface and TriggerContext methods\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/windows/TimeWindow.java` — Analyzed TimeWindow structure (start, end, maxTimestamp)\n\n## Dependency Chain\n\n1. **Define TradingSessionExtractor interface** — Functional interface, models SessionWindowTimeGapExtractor\n2. **Implement PricingSessionWindow assigner** — Extends MergingWindowAssigner<Object, TimeWindow>, calculates session boundaries based on trading hours\n3. **Implement PricingSessionTrigger** — Extends Trigger<Object, TimeWindow>, fires at market close\n4. **Integration** — Both components work together using EventTimeTrigger.create() pattern and TimeWindow.mergeWindows()\n\n## Architecture Notes\n\n### Window Assignment Strategy\n- **Input**: Market ID, timezone, open/close times (LocalTime)\n- **Processing**: For each element timestamp, determine which trading session it belongs to\n- **Output**: TimeWindow with session open/close timestamps\n- **Merging**: Delegates to TimeWindow.mergeWindows() for handling overlapping windows\n\n### Trigger Strategy\n- Fires when watermark passes window.maxTimestamp() (end of trading session)\n- Supports configurable early firing (circuit breaker events)\n- Implements canMerge() = true and onMerge() for session window compatibility\n- Clears event-time timers on window destruction\n\n## Implementation Strategy\n\n### PricingSessionExtractor (Functional Interface)\n```\nSignature: long extract(T element)\nPurpose: Extract market identifier from stream elements\nPackage: org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.assigners\nFollows: SessionWindowTimeGapExtractor pattern\n```\n\n### PricingSessionWindow (MergingWindowAssigner)\n```\nConstructor: PricingSessionWindow(String marketId, ZoneId timezone, LocalTime open, LocalTime close)\nKey Methods:\n- assignWindows(): Calculate TimeWindow for given element timestamp\n- getDefaultTrigger(): Return EventTimeTrigger.create()\n- mergeWindows(): Delegate to TimeWindow.mergeWindows()\n- getWindowSerializer(): Return new TimeWindow.Serializer()\n- isEventTime(): Return true\n\nHelper Method:\n- forMarket(String marketId, ZoneId timezone, LocalTime open, LocalTime close): Static factory\n\nLogic:\n1. Convert element timestamp to trading session date in market timezone\n2. Create window boundaries: [sessionStart, sessionEnd]\n3. Handle overnight sessions (e.g., futures markets)\n4. Return window as single-element collection\n```\n\n### PricingSessionTrigger (Trigger)\n```\nConstructor: Private, accessed via create() static method\nKey Methods:\n- onElement(): Register timer for window.maxTimestamp() if watermark not past\n- onEventTime(): Fire when time == window.maxTimestamp()\n- onProcessingTime(): Continue (event-time only)\n- clear(): Delete registered event-time timer\n- canMerge(): Return true\n- onMerge(): Re-register timer if watermark hasn't passed merged window end\n\nLogic:\n- Extends EventTimeTrigger pattern\n- Fires at session end when watermark arrives\n- Supports configurable early triggers via overridable onElement()\n```\n\n## Key Design Decisions\n\n1. **Using TimeWindow**: Maintains compatibility with existing Flink infrastructure, merging logic, serialization\n2. **Event-Time Based**: Financial trading operates on event time (market time), not processing time\n3. **Extending MergingWindowAssigner**: Allows overlapping session windows to be merged automatically\n4. **Delegating Merge to TimeWindow.mergeWindows()**: Reuses robust existing merge logic\n5. **EventTimeTrigger Pattern**: Simple, proven trigger strategy that fires at session boundaries\n6. **Factory Method**: Provides clean API (PricingSessionWindow.forMarket(...))\n\n## Testing Approach\n- Verify window assignment for various market timezones (NYSE, LSE, Asia-Pacific)\n- Test overnight session handling (futures markets)\n- Verify window merging behavior with overlapping sessions\n- Test trigger firing at session boundaries\n- Validate watermark handling and late-arriving elements\n\n## Code Changes\n\n### flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/TradingSessionExtractor.java\n```java\n/*\n * Licensed to the Apache Software Foundation (ASF) under one\n * or more contributor license agreements.  See the NOTICE file\n * distributed with this work for additional information\n * regarding copyright ownership.  The ASF licenses this file\n * to you under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the\n * \"License\"); you may not use this file except in compliance\n * with the License.  You may obtain a copy of the License at\n *\n *     http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0\n *\n * Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software\n * distributed under the License is distributed on an \"AS IS\" BASIS,\n * WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.\n * See the License for the specific language governing permissions and\n * limitations under the License.\n */\n\npackage org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.assigners;\n\nimport org.apache.flink.annotation.PublicEvolving;\n\nimport java.io.Serializable;\n\n/**\n * A {@code TradingSessionExtractor} extracts market identifiers from stream elements for dynamic\n * trading session window assignment.\n *\n * @param <T> The type of elements from which market identifiers can be extracted.\n */\n@PublicEvolving\npublic interface TradingSessionExtractor<T> extends Serializable {\n    /**\n     * Extracts the market identifier from the input element.\n     *\n     * @param element The input element.\n     * @return The market identifier (e.g., \"NYSE\", \"LSE\") for determining the trading session.\n     */\n    String extractMarketId(T element);\n}\n```\n\n### flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/PricingSessionWindow.java\n```java\n/*\n * Licensed to the Apache Software Foundation (ASF) under one\n * or more contributor license agreements.  See the NOTICE file\n * distributed with this work for additional information\n * regarding copyright ownership.  The ASF licenses this file\n * to you under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the\n * \"License\"); you may not use this file except in compliance\n * with the License.  You may obtain a copy of the License at\n *\n *     http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0\n *\n * Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software\n * distributed under the License is distributed on an \"AS IS\" BASIS,\n * WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.\n * See the License for the specific language governing permissions and\n * limitations under the License.\n */\n\npackage org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.assigners;\n\nimport org.apache.flink.annotation.PublicEvolving;\nimport org.apache.flink.api.common.ExecutionConfig;\nimport org.apache.flink.api.common.typeutils.TypeSerializer;\nimport org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.triggers.EventTimeTrigger;\nimport org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.triggers.Trigger;\nimport org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.windows.TimeWindow;\n\nimport java.time.LocalTime;\nimport java.time.ZoneId;\nimport java.time.ZonedDateTime;\nimport java.util.Collection;\nimport java.util.Collections;\n\n/**\n * A {@link WindowAssigner} that windows trading events into sessions based on market trading\n * hours. Windows are defined by market open and close times, allowing for session-based\n * aggregations in financial streaming applications.\n */\n@PublicEvolving\npublic class PricingSessionWindow extends MergingWindowAssigner<Object, TimeWindow> {\n    private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;\n\n    private final String marketId;\n    private final ZoneId timezone;\n    private final LocalTime sessionOpen;\n    private final LocalTime sessionClose;\n\n    protected PricingSessionWindow(\n            String marketId, ZoneId timezone, LocalTime sessionOpen, LocalTime sessionClose) {\n        if (marketId == null || marketId.isEmpty()) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Market ID cannot be null or empty\");\n        }\n        if (timezone == null) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Timezone cannot be null\");\n        }\n        if (sessionOpen == null || sessionClose == null) {\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Session open and close times cannot be null\");\n        }\n\n        this.marketId = marketId;\n        this.timezone = timezone;\n        this.sessionOpen = sessionOpen;\n        this.sessionClose = sessionClose;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Collection<TimeWindow> assignWindows(\n            Object element, long timestamp, WindowAssignerContext context) {\n        // Convert timestamp to market timezone\n        ZonedDateTime eventDateTime = ZonedDateTime.ofInstant(\n                java.time.Instant.ofEpochMilli(timestamp), timezone);\n\n        // Calculate session start and end timestamps\n        ZonedDateTime sessionStartZdt =\n                eventDateTime.toLocalDate().atTime(sessionOpen).atZone(timezone);\n        ZonedDateTime sessionEndZdt =\n                eventDateTime.toLocalDate().atTime(sessionClose).atZone(timezone);\n\n        long sessionStartMs = sessionStartZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n        long sessionEndMs = sessionEndZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n\n        // If event is before session open, assign to previous session\n        if (timestamp < sessionStartMs) {\n            sessionStartZdt = sessionStartZdt.minusDays(1);\n            sessionEndZdt = sessionEndZdt.minusDays(1);\n            sessionStartMs = sessionStartZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n            sessionEndMs = sessionEndZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n        }\n        // If event is after session close, assign to next session\n        else if (timestamp >= sessionEndMs) {\n            sessionStartZdt = sessionStartZdt.plusDays(1);\n            sessionEndZdt = sessionEndZdt.plusDays(1);\n            sessionStartMs = sessionStartZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n            sessionEndMs = sessionEndZdt.toInstant().toEpochMilli();\n        }\n\n        return Collections.singletonList(new TimeWindow(sessionStartMs, sessionEndMs));\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Trigger<Object, TimeWindow> getDefaultTrigger() {\n        return EventTimeTrigger.create();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        return String.format(\n                \"PricingSessionWindow(%s, %s, %s-%s)\",\n                marketId, timezone, sessionOpen, sessionClose);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a new {@code PricingSessionWindow} that assigns elements to sessions based on a\n     * fixed market's trading hours.\n     *\n     * @param marketId The market identifier (e.g., \"NYSE\", \"LSE\")\n     * @param timezone The timezone in which the market operates\n     * @param open The market opening time\n     * @param close The market closing time\n     * @return The window assigner\n     */\n    public static PricingSessionWindow forMarket(\n            String marketId, ZoneId timezone, LocalTime open, LocalTime close) {\n        return new PricingSessionWindow(marketId, timezone, open, close);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public TypeSerializer<TimeWindow> getWindowSerializer(ExecutionConfig executionConfig) {\n        return new TimeWindow.Serializer();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean isEventTime() {\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    /** Merge overlapping {@link TimeWindow}s. */\n    @Override\n    public void mergeWindows(\n            Collection<TimeWindow> windows, MergingWindowAssigner.MergeCallback<TimeWindow> c) {\n        TimeWindow.mergeWindows(windows, c);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/triggers/PricingSessionTrigger.java\n```java\n/*\n * Licensed to the Apache Software Foundation (ASF) under one\n * or more contributor license agreements.  See the NOTICE file\n * distributed with this work for additional information\n * regarding copyright ownership.  The ASF licenses this file\n * to you under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the\n * \"License\"); you may not use this file except in compliance\n * with the License.  You may obtain a copy of the License at\n *\n *     http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0\n *\n * Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software\n * distributed under the License is distributed on an \"AS IS\" BASIS,\n * WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.\n * See the License for the specific language governing permissions and\n * limitations under the License.\n */\n\npackage org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.triggers;\n\nimport org.apache.flink.annotation.PublicEvolving;\nimport org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.windows.TimeWindow;\n\n/**\n * A {@link Trigger} that fires when the market close time is reached (watermark passes the end of\n * the trading session window). This trigger is designed for use with {@link\n * org.apache.flink.streaming.api.windowing.assigners.PricingSessionWindow} to fire trading\n * session aggregations at market close.\n */\n@PublicEvolving\npublic class PricingSessionTrigger extends Trigger<Object, TimeWindow> {\n    private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;\n\n    private PricingSessionTrigger() {}\n\n    @Override\n    public TriggerResult onElement(\n            Object element, long timestamp, TimeWindow window, TriggerContext ctx)\n            throws Exception {\n        if (window.maxTimestamp() <= ctx.getCurrentWatermark()) {\n            return TriggerResult.FIRE;\n        } else {\n            ctx.registerEventTimeTimer(window.maxTimestamp());\n            return TriggerResult.CONTINUE;\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public TriggerResult onEventTime(long time, TimeWindow window, TriggerContext ctx) {\n        return time == window.maxTimestamp() ? TriggerResult.FIRE : TriggerResult.CONTINUE;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public TriggerResult onProcessingTime(long time, TimeWindow window, TriggerContext ctx)\n            throws Exception {\n        return TriggerResult.CONTINUE;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void clear(TimeWindow window, TriggerContext ctx) throws Exception {\n        ctx.deleteEventTimeTimer(window.maxTimestamp());\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean canMerge() {\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void onMerge(TimeWindow window, OnMergeContext ctx) {\n        long windowMaxTimestamp = window.maxTimestamp();\n        if (windowMaxTimestamp > ctx.getCurrentWatermark()) {\n            ctx.registerEventTimeTimer(windowMaxTimestamp);\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        return \"PricingSessionTrigger()\";\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a pricing session trigger that fires when the watermark passes the end of the\n     * trading session window.\n     *\n     * @return A new PricingSessionTrigger instance\n     */\n    public static PricingSessionTrigger create() {\n        return new PricingSessionTrigger();\n    }\n}\n```\n\n## pattern\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/WindowAssigner.java` — Understood base class interface requirements\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/MergingWindowAssigner.java` — Analyzed mergeWindows() callback pattern\n-
